---
title: "Numerical algorithms, optimisation, and computer performance: a selection of research from 2020"
categories:
- Parallel computing
- Linear algebra
reference: literature-2020
excerpt: "I won't bore you with clichés about how weird and difficult this year has been. Instead, I'd like to point out straightaway how large this year's selection of papers is: more than 400 papers, which is more than twice the papers I selected last year."
comments: true
---

I won't bore you with clichés about how weird and difficult this year has been. Instead, I'd like to point out straightaway how large this year's selection of papers is: more than 400 papers, which is more than twice the papers I selected last year.

This year, I haven't changed my Google Scholar query:

```
algorithm sparse method parallel performance matrix numerical optimization graph
```
but I have added some more supplemental papers, as I found fit.

In the coming year, I expect to add some papers about *Computational Sustainability*, a field I'm getting very interested in.

### Some general trends

* This year, I found several papers about more or less "classic" mathematical optimisation applied to machine learning and deep learning. To me, this was quite predictable, but it's always good to see how powerful and applicable some of those "classic" techniques are.
* Multi-precision algorithms are continuing to grow in popularity in the field of numerical analysis. The idea behind these algorithms is already very in deep learning.
Since we have 400 papers this year, I'm going to get some help from machine learning to analyse the data further.

### An analysis of the data

<div class="rtcContent"><div class="S1"><span>Load data and fit LDA model to find the topics.</span></div><div class="CodeBlock"><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S2"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>rng(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'default'</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>textData = string(fileread(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"bibliography.txt"</span><span>));</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>textData = splitlines(textData);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>textData = iCleanBibliographyText(textData);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>documents = iPrepareDocument(textData);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S4"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>[bagTraining, docsTest] = iSplitTrainingTest(documents, 0.8);</span></span></div></div></div><div class="S1"><span>Train a number of models, changing the number of topics.</span></div><div class="CodeBlock"><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S2"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>allNumTopics = 2:20;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>sizeAllNumTopics = numel(allNumTopics);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>mdl = cell(sizeAllNumTopics, 1);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>logProbabilities = cell(sizeAllNumTopics, 1);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>meanLogProbabilities = zeros(sizeAllNumTopics, 1);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>perplexities = cell(sizeAllNumTopics, 1);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>meanPerplexities = zeros(sizeAllNumTopics, 1);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">for </span><span>k = 1:sizeAllNumTopics</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    rng(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'default'</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    numTopics = allNumTopics(k);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    mdl{k} = fitlda(bagTraining, numTopics, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'Verbose'</span><span>, 0);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    logProbabilities{k} = logp(mdl{k}, bagTraining, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'NumSamples'</span><span>, 200);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    [~, perplexities{k}] = logp(mdl{k}, docsTest, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'NumSamples'</span><span>, 200);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    meanLogProbabilities(k) = mean(logProbabilities{k});</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    meanPerplexities(k) = mean(perplexities{k});</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S4"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div></div><div class="S1"><span>Compare the models, plot log-probabilities over the training set and perplexities over the test set.</span></div><div class="CodeBlock"><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S2"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>figure;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>title(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Model comparison"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>subplot(1, 2, 1);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>plot(allNumTopics, meanLogProbabilities);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>ylabel(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Log-probability on the training set"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>xlabel(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Number of topics"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>subplot(1, 2, 2);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>plot(allNumTopics, meanPerplexities);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>ylabel(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Perplexities on the training set"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper outputs"><div class="S5"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>xlabel(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Number of topics"</span><span>);</span></span></div><div class="S6"><div class="inlineElement eoOutputWrapper embeddedOutputsFigure" style="width: 100%; height: auto;"></div></div></div></div></div></div></div><h3 class="S8"><span>Helper functions</span></h3><div class="CodeBlock"><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S2"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">function </span><span>cleanDocuments = iCleanBibliographyText(document)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% Clean the input array of strings, making sure each string</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% corresponds to a bibliography entry.</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    stringSizes = strlength(document);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    document(stringSizes==0) = [];</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    isAbstract = contains(document, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Abstract:"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    idxAbstract = find(isAbstract);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% Previous abstract ends two rows before the new.</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    idxEndAbstract = [idxAbstract-2; numel(document)];</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    idxEndAbstract(1) = [];</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    cleanDocuments = repmat(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">""</span><span>, [numel(idxAbstract), 1]);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% Select each abstract</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">for </span><span>k = 1:numel(idxAbstract)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        currAbstractStart = idxAbstract(k);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        currAbstractEnd = idxEndAbstract(k);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        cleanDocuments(k) = join(document(currAbstractStart:currAbstractEnd));</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    cleanDocuments(strlength(cleanDocuments)==0 | ismissing(cleanDocuments)) = [];</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">function </span><span>documents = iPrepareDocument(textData)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% Prepare the document for analysis</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    documents = tokenizedDocument(textData);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    documents = removeStopWords(documents);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    documents = erasePunctuation(documents);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    documents = removeShortWords(documents, 2);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    documents = removeWords(documents, [</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Abstract"</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"2020"</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"arXiv"</span><span>]);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    documents = normalizeWords(documents, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'Style'</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'lemma'</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">function </span><span>iDisplayTopics(</span><span class="nonlocalVariableHighlighting">mdl</span><span>)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% Display the topics in the model</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    figure</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    numTopics = </span><span class="nonlocalVariableHighlighting">mdl</span><span>.NumTopics;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">for </span><span>idxTopic = 1:numTopics</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        topicWords = join(iFindTopicWords(idxTopic), </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">" "</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        disp(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Topic " </span><span>+ idxTopic + </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">": " </span><span>+ topicWords);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">function </span><span>words = iFindTopicWords(idxTopic)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        wordProbabilities = </span><span class="nonlocalVariableHighlighting">mdl</span><span>.TopicWordProbabilities(:, idxTopic);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        wordList = </span><span class="nonlocalVariableHighlighting">mdl</span><span>.Vocabulary;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        [~, idxTopProbabilities] = maxk(wordProbabilities, 10);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>        words = wordList(idxTopProbabilities);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">function </span><span>iDisplayTopicMixtures(topicMixtures, numTopics)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: log-probabilities"</span><span>)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">function </span><span>iDisplayClosenness(allTopicMixtures)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% Display the closenness between</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    topicNorms = vecnorm(allTopicMixtures, 2);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    numTopics = numel(topicNorms);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    topicCloseness = (allTopicMixtures')*(allTopicMixtures)./((topicNorms')*topicNorms);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    figure    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    currCol = pcolor(topicCloseness);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    colorbar(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'location'</span><span>, </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'EastOutside'</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    xlabel(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Topic number"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    ylabel(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Topic number"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    title(</span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">"Closeness between topics"</span><span>);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    plotAxis = currCol.Parent;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    plotAxis.XTick = 1:numTopics;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    plotAxis.YTick = 1:numTopics;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    plotAxis.YDir = </span><span style="color: rgb(170, 4, 249);">'reverse'</span><span>;</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    pbaspect(plotAxis, [1, 1, 1]);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">function </span><span>[bagTraining, docsTest] = iSplitTrainingTest(documents, ratio)</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    </span><span style="color: rgb(2, 128, 9);">% Split training set and test set</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    numDocuments = numel(documents);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    numTraining = round(ratio*numDocuments);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    documents = documents(randperm(numDocuments));</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    bagTraining = bagOfWords(documents(1:numTraining));</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S3"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span>    docsTest = documents(numTraining+1:end);</span></span></div></div><div class="inlineWrapper"><div class="S4"><span style="white-space: pre;"><span style="color: rgb(14, 0, 255);">end</span></span></div></div></div></div>

From the data analysis, I see:

* among the list of papers, the topic of numerical methods applied to tensors occurred a couple of times (topic 15 in my analysis). This is most likely a new trend that I'd like to keep an eye on, even if I don't know much about tensors;
* reading more about the topic of error analysis for multi-precision algorithms (topic 17 in my analysis) matched what I expected from last year's post;
* the topic of matrix partitioning for parallel algorithms and distribution of matrix blocks (topic 8 in my analysis) is still occurring in my selection;
* sparsity isn't occurring that much in the papers anymore. In practice, it's in only in one of the topics/subtopics my analysis identified (topic 13). This might be because the papers in the selection have increased, but not the papers in this area.
